    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg f5" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Features</h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Individual page for assignments, lectures, course material, course schedule</li>
<li>Auto generated Course schedule Page</li>
<li>Auto generated course updates section (for each new lectures and assignments) + custom/manual announcements</li>
<li>Super lightweight</li>
<li>Highly customizable</li>
<li>Ready to be used in Github Pages</li>
<li>Responsive Mobile View</li>
<li>Support for Google Analytics</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-change-log" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#change-log"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Change log</h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Version 2.0
<ul dir="auto">
<li>New Schedule page with more efficient use of space.</li>
<li>Gregorian calendar is now the default one (English Calendar).</li>
<li>Add customization options to home, assignments, lectures, and schedule pages.</li>
<li>Add support for themes (so you can modify the website's look according to your school's brandings)!.</li>
<li>Move navigation menus to YAML which means it is now easier to add new pages.</li>
<li>Add more flexibility to lecture's links</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-demo" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#demo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Demo</h1>
<p dir="auto">Checkout for a working demo at <a href="https://kazemnejad.github.io/jekyll-course-website-template/" rel="nofollow">kazemnejad.github.io/jekyll-course-website-template/</a>. You may also want to see this real-world example at <a href="https://iust-deep-learning.github.io/972/" rel="nofollow">iust-deep-learning.github.io/972</a> or <a href="https://iust-courses.github.io/ai97/" rel="nofollow">iust-courses.github.io/ai97/</a> (Please note the last two examples are using the older version).</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-some-screenshots" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#some-screenshots"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Some Screenshots</h1>

<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-acknowledgement" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#acknowledgement"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Acknowledgement</h1>
<p dir="auto">This template is heavily based on <a href="https://github.com/svmiller/course-website">svmiller / course-website</a>.</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-to-deploy-your-own-website-on-github-pages" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-deploy-your-own-website-on-github-pages"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>How to deploy your own website (on GitHub pages)</h1>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Fork this repository.</li>
<li>Open <code>_config.yml</code>.
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Update <code>url</code> field according to your GitHub account (e.g., <code>https://&lt;your-github-username&gt;.github.io/</code>).</li>
<li>Update <code>baseurl</code> field according to your reporsitory's name (e.g., <code>/cs101</code>).</li>
<li>Commit and push your changes.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>Go to your repository's settigns (<code>https://github.com/&lt;your-github-username&gt;/&lt;your-repo-name&gt;/settings</code>).</li>
<li>On GitHub Pages section, choose source to be your master branch, and enable Github Pages.</li>
<li>You are now ready to go! Start customizing your website.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Pro Tip: You don't need to clone your repo to update your website. Use GitHub web UI to update its source files, and GitHub will build and deploy your website automatically!</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Best Practice for managing repositories</strong>: If you plan to use this template for university courses, and the course is offered for multiple semesters/quarters, I suggests you to create a GitHub account or an Organization for it. Then, create new repoository under that account/organization for each semester.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Example:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Course name: CS101</li>
<li>Semester: Fall 2020</li>
<li>School name: CMU</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>=&gt; account/org name: <code>cmu-cs101</code></li>
<li>=&gt; repo name: <code>fa2020</code></li>
<li>=&gt; website address will be: <code>https://cmu-cs101.github.io/fa2020/</code></li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-to-test-your-website-locally" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-test-your-website-locally"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>How to test your website locally</h1>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Install Jekyll (<a href="https://jekyllrb.com/docs/installation/" rel="nofollow">Installation guide</a>)</li>
<li>Clone your repo</li>
<li>Watch your website while editing: <code>bundle exec jekyll serve</code></li>
</ol>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-to-customize" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-customize"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>How to customize</h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-changing-the-names" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#changing-the-names"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Changing the names</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Open <code>_config.yml</code></li>
<li>Update <code>course_name</code>, <code>course_semester</code>, and <code>course_description</code> (this will appear in the home page).</li>
<li>Update <code>schoolname</code>, <code>schoolurl</code>, <code>twitter_username</code>, and <code>address</code> accordingly.</li>
<li>(Optional) Enter your Google Analytics tracking ID in the <code>google_analytics</code> field (Remember to uncomment it).</li>
<li>Add more content to your home page: Update <code>index.md</code> (it supports Markdown!)</li>
<li>Update course staff info at <code>_data/people.yml</code> (You may need to upload the profile pics to <code>_images</code> folder.</li>
<li>(Optional) Open <code>_data/previous_offering.yml</code> and update the data if needed.</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-change-the-looks" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#change-the-looks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Change the looks</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Open <code>_sass/_user_vars.scss</code></li>
<li>Select your favorite from the pre-defined themes (comment all other themes, and uncomment your desired one)</li>
<li>Here are all themes:</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kazemnejad/jekyll-course-website-template/master/_images/screenshots/themes.png"><img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kazemnejad/jekyll-course-website-template/master/_images/screenshots/themes.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You can also change the colors manually to match your branding</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-contents" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#contents"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Contents</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-lectures" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#lectures"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Lectures</h3>
<p dir="auto">To add a new lecture, create an empty file with <code>.md</code> postfix in <code>_lectures/</code> directory. fill it using below template:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gfm notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
type: lecture
date: 20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30 
title: &lt;Title of this lecture&gt;

# optional
# please use /static_files/notes directory to store notes
thumbnail: /static_files/path/to/image.jpg

# optional
tldr: &quot;What is AI? How does it impact our lives? The current state of the art.&quot;
  
# optional
# set it to true if you dont want this lecture to appear in the updates section
hide_from_announcments: false

# optional
links: 
    - url: /static_files/presentations/lec.zip
      name: notes
    - url: /static_files/presentations/code.zip
      name: codes
    - url: https://google.com
      name: slides
    - url: https://example.com
      name: other
---
&lt;!-- Other additional contents using markdown --&gt;
**Suggested Readings:**
- [Readings 1](http://example.com)
- [Readings 2](http://example.com)"><pre><span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">lecture</span>
<span class="pl-ent">date</span>: <span class="pl-s">20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30 </span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;Title of this lecture&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> please use /static_files/notes directory to store notes</span>
<span class="pl-ent">thumbnail</span>: <span class="pl-s">/static_files/path/to/image.jpg</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-ent">tldr</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>What is AI? How does it impact our lives? The current state of the art.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> set it to true if you dont want this lecture to appear in the updates section</span>
<span class="pl-ent">hide_from_announcments</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-ent">links</span>: 
    - <span class="pl-ent">url</span>: <span class="pl-s">/static_files/presentations/lec.zip</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">notes</span>
    - <span class="pl-ent">url</span>: <span class="pl-s">/static_files/presentations/code.zip</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">codes</span>
    - <span class="pl-ent">url</span>: <span class="pl-s">https://google.com</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">slides</span>
    - <span class="pl-ent">url</span>: <span class="pl-s">https://example.com</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">other</span>
<span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">&lt;!--</span> Other additional contents using markdown <span class="pl-c">--&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-mb">**Suggested Readings:**</span>
<span class="pl-v">-</span> [<span class="pl-e">Readings 1</span>](http://example.com)
<span class="pl-v">-</span> [<span class="pl-e">Readings 2</span>](http://example.com)</pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-assignments" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#assignments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Assignments</h3>
<p dir="auto">To add a new assignments, create an empty file with <code>.md</code> postfix in <code>_assignments/</code> directory. fill it using below template:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gfm notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
type: assignment
date: 20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30
title: &lt;Assignment title (e.g. Assignment #1&gt;

# optional 
pdf: /static_files/assignments/assign_01.pdf

# optional
solutions: /static_files/assignments/assign_01_solutions.pdf

# optional
attachment: /static_files/assignments/assign_01_attachment.zip

# optional
# set it to true if you don't want this assignment to appear in the announcements section
hide_from_announcments: false

due_event: 
    type: due
    date: 20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30
    description: 'Assignment #1 due'
---
&lt;!-- Other additional contents using markdown --&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">assignment</span>
<span class="pl-ent">date</span>: <span class="pl-s">20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30</span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;Assignment title (e.g. Assignment </span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>1&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional </span>
<span class="pl-ent">pdf</span>: <span class="pl-s">/static_files/assignments/assign_01.pdf</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-ent">solutions</span>: <span class="pl-s">/static_files/assignments/assign_01_solutions.pdf</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> set it to true if you don't want this assignment to appear in the announcements section</span>
<span class="pl-ent">hide_from_announcments</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>

<span class="pl-ent">due_event</span>: 
    <span class="pl-ent">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">due</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">date</span>: <span class="pl-s">20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Assignment #1 due<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">&lt;!--</span> Other additional contents using markdown <span class="pl-c">--&gt;</span></span></pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dues--deadlines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dues--deadlines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Dues &amp; Deadlines</h3>
<p dir="auto">Use <code>_events/</code> directory to add new a deadline, use <code>type: due</code>. These events will apear at the schedule page.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gfm notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
type: due
date: 20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30
description: &lt;Description of deadline (e.g. 'Final report due')&gt;

# optional
# set it to true if you don't want this event to appear in the announcements section
hide_from_announcments: false
---"><pre><span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">due</span>
<span class="pl-ent">date</span>: <span class="pl-s">20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30</span>
<span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;Description of deadline (e.g. 'Final report due')&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> set it to true if you don't want this event to appear in the announcements section</span>
<span class="pl-ent">hide_from_announcments</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>
<span class="pl-c">---</span></pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-exams" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#exams"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Exams</h3>
<p dir="auto">Use <code>_events/</code> directory to add new Exam alert, use <code>type: exam</code>. These events will apear at the schedule page.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gfm notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
type: exam
date: 20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30
description: &lt;Description of the exam (e.g. 'The midterm exam')&gt;

# optional
# set it to true if you don't want to this event appear in the announcements section
hide_from_announcments: false
---"><pre><span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">exam</span>
<span class="pl-ent">date</span>: <span class="pl-s">20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30</span>
<span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;Description of the exam (e.g. 'The midterm exam')&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> set it to true if you don't want to this event appear in the announcements section</span>
<span class="pl-ent">hide_from_announcments</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>
<span class="pl-c">---</span></pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-custom-events" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#custom-events"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Custom Events</h3>
<p dir="auto">Use <code>_events/</code> directory to add new custom events, use <code>type: raw_event</code>. These events will apear at the schedule page.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gfm notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
type: raw_event
name: &lt;Event name&gt;
date: 20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30
description: &lt;Event description&gt;

# optional
# if you want to hide time in Schedule, set this to true
hide_time: false

# optional
# set it to true if you don't want this event appear to in the announcements section
hide_from_announcments: false
---
&lt;!-- you can create custom content using markdown. this section will be placed in &quot;Course Materials (in schedule section)&quot; --&gt;
## Hello
this is a custom event with `code` "><pre><span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">raw_event</span>
<span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;Event name&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-ent">date</span>: <span class="pl-s">20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30</span>
<span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;Event description&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> if you want to hide time in Schedule, set this to true</span>
<span class="pl-ent">hide_time</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> optional</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> set it to true if you don't want this event appear to in the announcements section</span>
<span class="pl-ent">hide_from_announcments</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>
<span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">&lt;!--</span> you can create custom content using markdown. this section will be placed in "Course Materials (in schedule section)" <span class="pl-c">--&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-mh"><span class="pl-mh">##</span><span class="pl-mh"> </span>Hello</span>
this is a custom event with <span class="pl-c1">`code`</span> </pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-updatesannouncements" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#updatesannouncements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Updates/Announcements</h3>
<p dir="auto">All contents here appear in at the home page
Use <code>_announcements/</code> directory to create new Announcement</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gfm notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
date: 20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30
---
&lt;put a short announcement here, you can use all markdown features&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">date</span>: <span class="pl-s">20xx-xx-xxTx:xx:xx+4:30</span>
<span class="pl-c">---</span>
&lt;put a short announcement here, you can use all markdown features&gt;</pre></div>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-advanced-customization" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#advanced-customization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Advanced Customization</h2>
<p dir="auto">You can add custom contents to each section (lectures, assignments, schedule, materials, and project)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Lectures: Edit <code>lectures.md</code></li>
<li>Assignments: Edit <code>assignments.md</code></li>
<li>Schedule: Edit <code>schedule.md</code></li>
<li>Materials: Edit <code>materials.md</code></li>
<li>Project: Edit <code>project.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Additionally, you can update navigation menus (the menu at the top of the website) by editing <code>_data/nav.yml</code></p>
<p dir="auto">To add new section, add new navigation menu. Then create a new file in website's root directory using the following template:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gfm notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
layout: page
title: Page Title
permalink: /page-address/
---"><pre><span class="pl-c">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">layout</span>: <span class="pl-s">page</span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Page Title</span>
<span class="pl-ent">permalink</span>: <span class="pl-s">/page-address/</span>
<span class="pl-c">---</span></pre></div>
</article>
  </div>
</div>
